ddX  1.0.0
Libary for domain-decomposition methods for polarizable continuum models
llgnew.f
1 c
2 c routine to generate the lebedev-laikov grid (g and w for the weights arrays)
3 c with the closest number of points from ng
4 c
5  subroutine llgrid(ngrid,w,grid)
6  implicit real*8 (a-h,o-z)
7  parameter(nllg=32,ngmax=5810)
8  integer n,igrid,i,ng0(nllg),inear,jnear,ig
9  real*8 w(*),grid(3,*), four
10  real*8 wtemp(ngmax),x(ngmax),y(ngmax),z(ngmax)
11  save one, four
12  data one/1.0d0/, four /4.0d0/
13 c
14  if (ngrid.eq.6) then
15  call ld0006(x,y,z,wtemp,n)
16  else if (ngrid.eq.14) then
17  call ld0014(x,y,z,wtemp,n)
18  else if (ngrid.eq.26) then
19  call ld0026(x,y,z,wtemp,n)
20  else if (ngrid.eq.38) then
21  call ld0038(x,y,z,wtemp,n)
22  else if (ngrid.eq.50) then
23  call ld0050(x,y,z,wtemp,n)
24  else if (ngrid.eq.74) then
25  call ld0074(x,y,z,wtemp,n)
26  else if (ngrid.eq.86) then
27  call ld0086(x,y,z,wtemp,n)
28  else if (ngrid.eq.110) then
29  call ld0110(x,y,z,wtemp,n)
30  else if (ngrid.eq.146) then
31  call ld0146(x,y,z,wtemp,n)
32  else if (ngrid.eq.170) then
33  call ld0170(x,y,z,wtemp,n)
34  else if (ngrid.eq.194) then
35  call ld0194(x,y,z,wtemp,n)
36  else if (ngrid.eq.230) then
37  call ld0230(x,y,z,wtemp,n)
38  else if (ngrid.eq.266) then
39  call ld0266(x,y,z,wtemp,n)
40  else if (ngrid.eq.302) then
41  call ld0302(x,y,z,wtemp,n)
42  else if (ngrid.eq.350) then
43  call ld0350(x,y,z,wtemp,n)
44  else if (ngrid.eq.434) then
45  call ld0434(x,y,z,wtemp,n)
46  else if (ngrid.eq.590) then
47  call ld0590(x,y,z,wtemp,n)
48  else if (ngrid.eq.770) then
49  call ld0770(x,y,z,wtemp,n)
50  else if (ngrid.eq.974) then
51  call ld0974(x,y,z,wtemp,n)
52  else if (ngrid.eq.1202) then
53  call ld1202(x,y,z,wtemp,n)
54  else if (ngrid.eq.1454) then
55  call ld1454(x,y,z,wtemp,n)
56  else if (ngrid.eq.1730) then
57  call ld1730(x,y,z,wtemp,n)
58  else if (ngrid.eq.2030) then
59  call ld2030(x,y,z,wtemp,n)
60  else if (ngrid.eq.2354) then
61  call ld2354(x,y,z,wtemp,n)
62  else if (ngrid.eq.2702) then
63  call ld2702(x,y,z,wtemp,n)
64  else if (ngrid.eq.3074) then
65  call ld3074(x,y,z,wtemp,n)
66  else if (ngrid.eq.3470) then
67  call ld3470(x,y,z,wtemp,n)
68  else if (ngrid.eq.3890) then
69  call ld3890(x,y,z,wtemp,n)
70  else if (ngrid.eq.4334) then
71  call ld4334(x,y,z,wtemp,n)
72  else if (ngrid.eq.4802) then
73  call ld4802(x,y,z,wtemp,n)
74  else if (ngrid.eq.5294) then
75  call ld5294(x,y,z,wtemp,n)
76  else if (ngrid.eq.5810) then
77  call ld5810(x,y,z,wtemp,n)
78  end if
79 c
80 c scaling because the weights are normalised and back to grid format
81 c
82  pi = four*atan(one)
83  do 20 i = 1, ngrid
84  w(i) = wtemp(i)*four*pi
85  grid(1,i) = x(i)
86  grid(2,i) = y(i)
87  grid(3,i) = z(i)
88  20 continue
89 c
90  return
91  end
92 
93  subroutine gen_oh(code, num, x, y, z, wtemp, a, b, v)
94  implicit logical(a-z)
95  real*8 x(*),y(*),z(*),wtemp(*)
96  double precision a,b,v
97  integer code
98  integer num
99  double precision c
100 chvd
101 chvd This subroutine is part of a set of subroutines that generate
102 chvd Lebedev grids [1-6] for integration on a sphere. The original
103 chvd C-code [1] was kindly provided by Dr. Dmitri N. Laikov and
104 chvd translated into fortran by Dr. Christoph van Wuellen.
105 chvd This subroutine was translated from C to fortran77 by hand.
106 chvd
107 chvd Users of this code are asked to include reference [1] in their
108 chvd publications, and in the user- and programmers-manuals
109 chvd describing their codes.
110 chvd
111 chvd This code was distributed through CCL (http://www.ccl.net/).
112 chvd
113 chvd [1] V.I. Lebedev, and D.N. Laikov
114 chvd "A quadrature formula for the sphere of the 131st
115 chvd algebraic order of accuracy"
116 chvd Doklady Mathematics, Vol. 59, No. 3, 1999, pp. 477-481.
117 chvd
118 chvd [2] V.I. Lebedev
119 chvd "A quadrature formula for the sphere of 59th algebraic
120 chvd order of accuracy"
121 chvd Russian Acad. Sci. Dokl. Math., Vol. 50, 1995, pp. 283-286.
122 chvd
123 chvd [3] V.I. Lebedev, and A.L. Skorokhodov
124 chvd "Quadrature formulas of orders 41, 47, and 53 for the sphere"
125 chvd Russian Acad. Sci. Dokl. Math., Vol. 45, 1992, pp. 587-592.
126 chvd
127 chvd [4] V.I. Lebedev
128 chvd "Spherical quadrature formulas exact to orders 25-29"
129 chvd Siberian Mathematical Journal, Vol. 18, 1977, pp. 99-107.
130 chvd
131 chvd [5] V.I. Lebedev
132 chvd "Quadratures on a sphere"
133 chvd Computational Mathematics and Mathematical Physics, Vol. 16,
134 chvd 1976, pp. 10-24.
135 chvd
136 chvd [6] V.I. Lebedev
137 chvd "Values of the nodes and weights of ninth to seventeenth
138 chvd order Gauss-Markov quadrature formulae invariant under the
139 chvd octahedron group with inversion"
140 chvd Computational Mathematics and Mathematical Physics, Vol. 15,
141 chvd 1975, pp. 44-51.
142 chvd
143 cvw
144 cvw Given a point on a sphere (specified by a and b), generate all
145 cvw the equivalent points under Oh symmetry, making grid points with
146 cvw weight v.
147 cvw The variable num is increased by the number of different points
148 cvw generated.
149 cvw
150 cvw Depending on code, there are 6...48 different but equivalent
151 cvw points.
152 cvw
153 cvw code=1: (0,0,1) etc ( 6 points)
154 cvw code=2: (0,a,a) etc, a=1/sqrt(2) ( 12 points)
155 cvw code=3: (a,a,a) etc, a=1/sqrt(3) ( 8 points)
156 cvw code=4: (a,a,b) etc, b=sqrt(1-2 a^2) ( 24 points)
157 cvw code=5: (a,b,0) etc, b=sqrt(1-a^2), a input ( 24 points)
158 cvw code=6: (a,b,c) etc, c=sqrt(1-a^2-b^2), a/b input ( 48 points)
159 cvw
160  goto (1,2,3,4,5,6) code
161  write (6,*) 'Gen_Oh: Invalid Code'
162  stop
163  1 continue
164  a=1.0d0
165  x(1) = a
166  y(1) = 0.0d0
167  z(1) = 0.0d0
168  wtemp(1) = v
169  x(2) = -a
170  y(2) = 0.0d0
171  z(2) = 0.0d0
172  wtemp(2) = v
173  x(3) = 0.0d0
174  y(3) = a
175  z(3) = 0.0d0
176  wtemp(3) = v
177  x(4) = 0.0d0
178  y(4) = -a
179  z(4) = 0.0d0
180  wtemp(4) = v
181  x(5) = 0.0d0
182  y(5) = 0.0d0
183  z(5) = a
184  wtemp(5) = v
185  x(6) = 0.0d0
186  y(6) = 0.0d0
187  z(6) = -a
188  wtemp(6) = v
189  num=num+6
190  return
191 cvw
192  2 continue
193  a=sqrt(0.5d0)
194  x( 1) = 0d0
195  y( 1) = a
196  z( 1) = a
197  wtemp( 1) = v
198  x( 2) = 0d0
199  y( 2) = -a

2970 chvd Lebedev grids [1-6] for integration on a sphere. The original
2971 chvd C-code [1] was kindly provided by Dr. Dmitri N. Laikov and
2972 chvd translated into fortran by Dr. Christoph van Wuellen.

2974 chvd tool written by Dr. Christoph van Wuellen.

3821 chvd Lebedev grids [1-6] for integration on a sphere. The original
3822 chvd C-code [1] was kindly provided by Dr. Dmitri N. Laikov and
3823 chvd translated into fortran by Dr. Christoph van Wuellen.

3825 chvd tool written by Dr. Christoph van Wuellen.

4156  SUBROUTINE ld3470(X,Y,Z,W,N)
4157  real*8 x(3470)
4158  real*8 y(3470)
4159  real*8 z(3470)
4160  real*8 w(3470)
4161  INTEGER N
4162  DOUBLE PRECISION A,B,V
4163 CVW
4164 CVW LEBEDEV 3470-POINT ANGULAR GRID
4165 CVW
4166 chvd
4167 chvd This subroutine is part of a set of subroutines that generate
4168 chvd Lebedev grids [1-6] for integration on a sphere. The original
4169 chvd C-code [1] was kindly provided by Dr. Dmitri N. Laikov and
4170 chvd translated into fortran by Dr. Christoph van Wuellen.
4171 chvd This subroutine was translated using a C to fortran77 conversion
4172 chvd tool written by Dr. Christoph van Wuellen.
4173 chvd
4174 chvd Users of this code are asked to include reference [1] in their
4175 chvd publications, and in the user- and programmers-manuals
4176 chvd describing their codes.
4177 chvd
4178 chvd This code was distributed through CCL (http://wtempwtempwtemp.ccl.net/).
4179 chvd

4181 chvd "A quadrature formula for the sphere of the 131st
4182 chvd algebraic order of accuracy"

4184 chvd

4538  SUBROUTINE ld3890(X,Y,Z,W,N)
4539  real*8 x(3890)
4540  real*8 y(3890)

4542  real*8 w(3890)

4544  DOUBLE PRECISION A,B,V
4545 CVW
4546 CVW LEBEDEV 3890-POINT ANGULAR GRID
4547 CVW
4548 chvd
4549 chvd This subroutine is part of a set of subroutines that generate
4550 chvd Lebedev grids [1-6] for integration on a sphere. The original
4551 chvd C-code [1] was kindly provided by Dr. Dmitri N. Laikov and
4552 chvd translated into fortran by Dr. Christoph van Wuellen.
4553 chvd This subroutine was translated using a C to fortran77 conversion
4554 chvd tool written by Dr. Christoph van Wuellen.
4555 chvd
4556 chvd Users of this code are asked to include reference [1] in their
4557 chvd publications, and in the user- and programmers-manuals
4558 chvd describing their codes.
4559 chvd
4560 chvd This code was distributed through CCL (http://wtempwtempwtemp.ccl.net/).
4561 chvd

4564 chvd algebraic order of accuracy"

4957  SUBROUTINE ld4334(X,Y,Z,W,N)
4958  real*8 x(4334)
4959  real*8 y(4334)

4965 CVW LEBEDEV 4334-POINT ANGULAR GRID
4966 CVW
4967 chvd
4968 chvd This subroutine is part of a set of subroutines that generate
4969 chvd Lebedev grids [1-6] for integration on a sphere. The original
4970 chvd C-code [1] was kindly provided by Dr. Dmitri N. Laikov and
4971 chvd translated into fortran by Dr. Christoph van Wuellen.
4972 chvd This subroutine was translated using a C to fortran77 conversion
4973 chvd tool written by Dr. Christoph van Wuellen.
4974 chvd

4976 chvd publications, and in the user- and programmers-manuals
4977 chvd describing their codes.
4978 chvd
4979 chvd This code was distributed through CCL (http://wtempwtempwtemp.ccl.net/).

4983 chvd algebraic order of accuracy"

5415  SUBROUTINE ld4802(X,Y,Z,W,N)

5425 chvd

5427 chvd Lebedev grids [1-6] for integration on a sphere. The original
5428 chvd C-code [1] was kindly provided by Dr. Dmitri N. Laikov and
5429 chvd translated into fortran by Dr. Christoph van Wuellen.

5431 chvd tool written by Dr. Christoph van Wuellen.

5914  SUBROUTINE ld5294(X,Y,Z,W,N)
5915  real*8 x(5294)
5916  real*8 y(5294)

5923 CVW
5924 chvd
5925 chvd This subroutine is part of a set of subroutines that generate
5926 chvd Lebedev grids [1-6] for integration on a sphere. The original
5927 chvd C-code [1] was kindly provided by Dr. Dmitri N. Laikov and
5928 chvd translated into fortran by Dr. Christoph van Wuellen.
5929 chvd This subroutine was translated using a C to fortran77 conversion
5930 chvd tool written by Dr. Christoph van Wuellen.
5931 chvd
5932 chvd Users of this code are asked to include reference [1] in their
5933 chvd publications, and in the user- and programmers-manuals
5934 chvd describing their codes.
5935 chvd
5936 chvd This code was distributed through CCL (http://wtempwtempwtemp.ccl.net/).
5937 chvd
